By 13, he had his own vocal group, the Bobbysoxers. He performed at every amateur night he could get to in his mothers car, unbeknownst to her of course. Soon after, he won a trip to New York by winning a Campbells soup contest for IGA Food Stores that required him to spend three months collecting soup can labels.
